 ek taraf kashmir ghati main pratibandh rahaa vahiin jammu ke log kush bataae ja rahe the to leh-ladakh ke ilaake main kushi ke saath logon ke dilon main ashankaayen bhi hai
 Everything is normal in Leh
 telephone or internet par koi pratibandh nahin he, bhale hi wo thodaa dhimaa he magar us par koi roak tok nahin he

 jammu kashmir ke punargathan ke baad ladakh main kargil kaa ilaaka bhi joda gaya he jo shiya muslim bahul ilaaka he
 At the same time, the remaining population of Ladakh belongs to Hindu and Buddhist people
 muslim aabaadi bhi acchhee taadaad main he
 Leh is the largest city of Ladakh and is also the district headquarters
 leh kii aabaadi mahaj dedh lakh he yani dilli ke kisi bade ilaake se bhi chota
 There is very little rain here
 ise barf kaa registan bhi kehete hai
 There is a water scarcity here and nothing rises and there is a lot of snowfall four to five times a year
 un dinon leh ladakh bharat ke baaqi hisson se cat jaataa he
 Many interesting issues emerged when talking to the people here

 People here want this area to be kept in Sindoor 6 (schedule 6 of Indian constitution)
 vaise bhi anusuchit jati ke rashtriya ayog ne bhi ladakh ko isamen shaamil kiye jane kii sifaarish kii hui he
 So far, places like Assam, Meghalaya, Mizoram, Tripura have been included in Sindoor 6
 darjeeling main bhi hill council he
 Estimates have the same arrangement
 sudur 6 main aane ke baad yahaan ke jila council zamin, jangal, pani, kheti jaise vishyon par kaanoon bana sakati he or yahi vajah he ki yahaan ke sthaneey logon kaa kahana he ki tourizam ke kshetra main bahari nivesh ko niyam banaakar niyantrit karnaa chahie
 The local people should control the land and hotels of the tourism sector
 yahaan ke log bade hotel chen ke aa jane ke baad apana dhandha band hone ke dar se ghabaraae hue hai
 They fear that if the big hotel chains come here then there will be no space left for them
 unka maananaa he zile main bade hotel chen kii zarurat nahin he
 At the same time, people definitely want big hospitals to open so that the people of Ladakh can get better treatment
 ab ye jila aspataal he jo kaafii behatar he magar us par boj bahut he

 isliye iske bhandaaran or sangrakshan kii zarurat he

 ab kargil bhi iskaa hissaa he

 bhartiya dand samhita yani ipisi kii dhara 503 ke tahat kisi ko dekh lene kii dhamkee dena krime he
 In doing so, a provision of jail sentence ranging from two years to seven years has been made under Section 506 of the IPC
 agar aap kisi ke sharir, pratishtha yaa sampatti ko nuksaan pahunchane kii dhamkee dete hai, to aapako do saal kii sajaa ho sakati he
 With this, you can be fined
 iske alaava agar aap kisi ko jaan se maarane yaa aag lagaakar kisi kii sampatti ko nuksaan pahunchane yaa phir kisi mahila ke charitra par laanchhan lagane kii dhamkee dete hai, to aapako saat saal tak kii sajaa ho sakati he
 According to Section 506 of the IPC, if a person threatens to commit an offense which is punishable by death or life imprisonment or imprisonment up to seven years, then the threater can be punished with imprisonment for seven years
 saath hi aisi dhamkee dene vaale par jurmaana lagaaya jayega
 However, it is not considered threatening for anyone to use profanity or abuse
 uttar pradesh or andhra pradesh rajya main to dekh lene kii dhamkee dene ko gaiyr jamaanti aparaadh banaaya he
 This means that if someone is threatened to be seen in Uttar Pradesh and Andhra Pradesh, it would be a non-bailable offense
 aisi dhamkee dene vaale ko nyaayalay se hi jamaanat milegi

 State of Uttar Pradesh, the Supreme Court had said that only abusive abuses cannot be considered a threat
